| <span data-ttu-id="21cf3-1491">進入</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="21cf3-1491">Entry</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="21cf3-1492">值</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="21cf3-1492">Value</span></span> |
